| **EMA 21** | 0.3797 | Above price – medium‑term downtrend |
| **EMA 50** | 0.3954 | Well above price – long‑term downtrend |
| **RSI 14** | 35.98 | Near oversold region (below 30 = oversold, 30‑40 = mildly bearish) |
| **ATR 14** | 0.009486 | Average true range; price moves ~0.0095 USDT per hour |
| **Volatility %** | 2.557 % | Recent 1‑h volatility |
| **Bollinger Bands** | Mid 0.3799, Upper 0.4064, Lower 0.3534 | Price sits just above the lower band, indicating possible support |
| **Trend Strength** | 0.25 (0‑1 scale) | Weak bullish/neutral trend |
| **Momentum Score** | 0.35 (0‑1) | Low momentum, leaning bearish |
| **Technical Score** | 0.257 (0‑1) | Overall technical outlook is weak |
| **Short Score** | 0.743 (0‑1) | Strong bias toward short positions |
| **Key Levels** | Support 0.3552, Resistance 0.4042, Pivot 0.3768 | Immediate support just below current price; resistance ~0.404 USDT |
| **Suggested Bias** | **short** | Model recommends a short (sell) stance |

### Key Insights for Decision‑Making
1. **Price is below all three EMAs** (9, 21, 50), confirming a bearish alignment across short‑, medium‑, and long‑term trends.  
2. **RSI at ~36** suggests the asset is approaching oversold territory but not yet there; a bounce is possible, yet the broader trend remains down.  
3. **Momentum and technical scores are low** (≈0.3), reinforcing weak upward pressure.  
4. **Short score is high (0.74)**, matching the suggested bias to go short.  
5. **Support at 0.3552** is ~0.0157 USDT below the current price; a break below this level could trigger a sharper move toward the lower Bollinger band.  
6. **Resistance at 0.4042** is ~0.0333 USDT above price; a rally to this level would be a sizable 8–9 % move, but current indicators do not support such upside.  

### Potential Trade Considerations
- **Entry:** Near current price (0.3709) or on a slight pull‑back to the support zone (≈0.355‑0.360).  
- **Stop‑Loss:** Tight, e.g., just above the recent swing high or above the EMA 9 (~0.375) to limit loss to ~1‑1.2 % as per profit doctrine.  
- **Target:** Aim for the next strong support or lower Bollinger band (~0.353) for a ~4‑5 % downside move, or a larger 5‑10 % move if price breaks cleanly below 0.3552.  

### Errors / Issues
- No errors were reported; the tool returned a complete technical analysis payload.  

---  

**Bottom line:** The technical snapshot for WLD‑USDT on the 1‑hour chart shows a clear bearish bias with price below key EMAs, low momentum, and a high short‑score. A short trade with a tight stop and a target of 3‑5 % downside aligns with the profit doctrine’s asymmetric payoff strategy.
